In the case where a label set is\\n58: transitioning from pending to firing the state of the alert instance is \\\"Firing\\\" and when transitioning from firing to\\n59: normal the state of the alert instance is \\\"Normal\\\".\\n60: \\n61: ### Which Alertmanager?\\n62: \\n63: In ngalert it is possible to send alerts to the internal Alertmanager, an external Alertmanager, or both.\\n64: \\n65: The internal Alertmanager is called `MultiOrgAlertmanager` and creates an Alertmanager for each organization in\\n66: Grafana to preserve isolation between organizations in Grafana. In the case where a label set is\n58: transitioning from pending to firing the state of the alert instance is \"Firing\" and when transitioning from firing to\n59: normal the state of the alert instance is \"Normal\".\n60: \n61: ### Which Alertmanager?\n62: \n63: In ngalert it is possible to send alerts to the internal Alertmanager, an external Alertmanager, or both.\n64: \n65: The internal Alertmanager is called `MultiOrgAlertmanager` and creates an Alertmanager for each organization in\n66: Grafana to preserve isolation between organizations in Grafana. The `MultiOrgAlertmanager` receives alerts from the\n67: scheduler and then forwards the alert to the correct Alertmanager for the organization.\n68: \n69: ... [chunk truncated]","endLine":81,"startLine":53},{"content":"20: \n21: ## Scheduling and evaluation of alert rules\n22: \n23: The scheduling of alert rules happens in the `schedule` package. This package is responsible for managing the evaluation\n24: of alert rules including checking for new alert rules and stopping the evaluation of deleted alert rules.\n25: \n26: The scheduler runs at a fixed interval, called its heartbeat, in which it does a number of tasks:\n27: \n28: 1. Fetch the alert rules for all organizations (excluding disabled)\n29: 2. Start a goroutine (if this is a new alert rule or the scheduler has just started) to evaluate the alert rule\n30: 3. \"pkg/services/ngalert/sender/router.go\", \"symbol\": \"NewAlertsRouter\"}\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"## Grafana Unified Alerting (ngalert) Architecture\\n\\nThe unified alerting subsystem in grafana/grafana comprises five major interacting components:\\n\\n### 1. Alert Rule Storage (pkg/services/ngalert/store/)\\nThe storage layer is implemented by `DBstore` (database.go), a database-backed storage system that persists alert rule definitions and metadata. Key files include:\\n- `database.go`: Main DBstore class implementing AlertingStore and rule persistence\\n- `alert_rule.go`: Methods for querying alert rules via GetAlertRulesForScheduling() and GetAlertRulesKeysForScheduling()\\n- `instance_database.go`: Stores alert instances (individual alert firing states) via SaveAlertInstances() and ListAlertInstances()\\n- `alertmanager.go`: Persists alertmanager configurations\\n\\nThe DBstore is injectable through ProvideDBStore() and serves as the single source of truth for all alert rule definitions across all organizations.\\n\\n### 2. Alert Rule Scheduler (pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/)\\nThe scheduler manages the periodic evaluation of alert rules. Key files:\\n- `schedule.go`: Main scheduler implementing ScheduleService interface, created via NewScheduler(). Manages the evaluation loop and rule registry\\n- `alert_rule.go`: Per-rule executor that runs in its own goroutine, fetches evaluation results and sends them to state manager\\n- `fetcher.go`: updateSchedulableAlertRules() fetches rules from DBstore at configured heartbeat intervals\\n- `recording_rule.go`: Handles recording rules (Prometheus-style rules that write metrics)\\n\\nThe scheduler runs as a continuous service (Run() method) that fetches all active rules, detects changes, and spawns/terminates evaluation goroutines. It uses the AlertsSender interface to dispatch firing alerts.\\n\\n### 3. State Manager (pkg/services/ngalert/state/)\\nThe state manager tracks alert states over time and determines state transitions. Core files:\\n- `manager.go`: Manager class managing alert state cache, created via NewManager(). Implements AlertInstanceManager for state queries\\n- `state.go`: State type representing individual alert instance state with fields like Firing, Pending, etc.\\n- `cache.go`: In-memory cache of all current alert states organized by rule and labels\\n- `persist.go`: StatePersister and Historian interfaces for persistence and history recording\\n- `store_state_reader.go`: StoreStateReader reads alert instances from database on startup\\n\\nThe Manager processes evaluation results via ProcessEvalResults(), compares against previous states to determine transitions (e.g., pending→firing), and records state changes. It maintains a cache warm-loaded from the database (Warm() method) and periodically persists state via StatePersister.\\n\\n### 4. Notifier (pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/)\\nThe notifier delivers alerts to alertmanager instances and manages silences. Key files:\\n- `alertmanager.go`: Per-organization alertmanager wrapper (alertmanager class, NewAlertmanager()). Wraps prometheus-alertmanager\\n- `multiorg_alertmanager.go`: MultiOrgAlertmanager created via NewMultiOrgAlertmanager(). Manages per-org alertmanagers and routes alerts to correct org\\n- `receiver_svc.go`: ReceiverService manages notification receiver configuration per organization\\n- `silence_svc.go`: SilenceService manages active silences that suppress alerts\\n\\nWhen scheduler dispatches alerts, they flow through MultiOrgAlertmanager which routes them to the correct per-org alertmanager. The alertmanager applies routing rules, silences, and notification policies before sending notifications.\\n\\n### 5. History Writer (pkg/services/ngalert/state/historian/)\\nThe historian records state transitions for audit and querying. Implementation files:\\n- `core.go`: WriteStateTransition() base function for recording state changes with rule metadata\\n- `annotation.go`: AnnotationBackend uses Grafana annotations as backing store\\n- `prometheus.go`: PrometheusWriter writes state history to Prometheus remote write endpoint\\n- `loki.go`: LokiWriter writes state history to Loki\\n- `multiple.go`: MultipleBackend supports multiple simultaneous backends (e.g., primary Loki + secondary Prometheus)\\n- `backend.go`: Backend type abstraction allowing selection between annotation/prometheus/loki\\n\\nThe Historian interface (persist.go) is called by state manager's persistence layer to Record() state transitions. Multiple backends can be active simultaneously, with one designated as primary for reads.\\n\\n### 6. Alert Sender (pkg/services/ngalert/sender/)\\nThe sender routes evaluated alerts to external systems. Key files:\\n- `router.go`: AlertsRouter created via NewAlertsRouter(). Routes alerts to internal MultiOrgAlertmanager and/or external alertmanagers based on admin configuration\\n- `notifier.go`: ExternalAlertmanagerSender sends alerts to external alertmanagers\\n- `sender.go`: Base sender functionality\\n\\nThe router is called by scheduler with alert transitions and determines whether to send to: (1) internal alertmanager, (2) external alertmanager, or (3) both, based on configuration stored in AdminConfigurationStore.\\n\\n### 7. grafana/grafana comprises five major interacting components:\\n\\n### 1. Alert Rule Storage (pkg/services/ngalert/store/)\\nThe storage layer is implemented by `DBstore` (database.go), a database-backed storage system that persists alert rule definitions and metadata. Key files include:\\n- `database.go`: Main DBstore class implementing AlertingStore and rule persistence\\n- `alert_rule.go`: Methods for querying alert rules via GetAlertRulesForScheduling() and GetAlertRulesKeysForScheduling()\\n- `instance_database.go`: Stores alert instances (individual alert firing states) via SaveAlertInstances() and ListAlertInstances()\\n- `alertmanager.go`: Persists alertmanager configurations\\n\\nThe DBstore is injectable through ProvideDBStore() and serves as the single source of truth for all alert rule definitions across all organizations.\\n\\n### 2. Alert Rule Scheduler (pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/)\\nThe scheduler manages the periodic evaluation of alert rules. Key files:\\n- `schedule.go`: Main scheduler implementing ScheduleService interface, created via NewScheduler(). Manages the evaluation loop and rule registry\\n- `alert_rule.go`: Per-rule executor that runs in its own goroutine, fetches evaluation results and sends them to state manager\\n- `fetcher.go`: updateSchedulableAlertRules() fetches rules from DBstore at configured heartbeat intervals\\n- `recording_rule.go`: Handles recording rules (Prometheus-style rules that write metrics)\\n\\nThe scheduler runs as a continuous service (Run() method) that fetches all active rules, detects changes, and spawns/terminates evaluation goroutines. It uses the AlertsSender interface to dispatch firing alerts.\\n\\n### 3. State Manager (pkg/services/ngalert/state/)\\nThe state manager tracks alert states over time and determines state transitions. Core files:\\n- `manager.go`: Manager class managing alert state cache, created via NewManager(). Implements AlertInstanceManager for state queries\\n- `state.go`: State type representing individual alert instance state with fields like Firing, Pending, etc.\\n- `cache.go`: In-memory cache of all current alert states organized by rule and labels\\n- `persist.go`: StatePersister and Historian interfaces for persistence and history recording\\n- `store_state_reader.go`: StoreStateReader reads alert instances from database on startup\\n\\nThe Manager processes evaluation results via ProcessEvalResults(), compares against previous states to determine transitions (e.g., pending→firing), and records state changes. It maintains a cache warm-loaded from the database (Warm() method) and periodically persists state via StatePersister.\\n\\n### 4. Notifier (pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/)\\nThe notifier delivers alerts to alertmanager instances and manages silences. Key files:\\n- `alertmanager.go`: Per-organization alertmanager wrapper (alertmanager class, NewAlertmanager()). Wraps prometheus-alertmanager\\n- `multiorg_alertmanager.go`: MultiOrgAlertmanager created via NewMultiOrgAlertmanager(). Manages per-org alertmanagers and routes alerts to correct org\\n- `receiver_svc.go`: ReceiverService manages notification receiver configuration per organization\\n- `silence_svc.go`: SilenceService manages active silences that suppress alerts\\n\\nWhen scheduler dispatches alerts, they flow through MultiOrgAlertmanager which routes them to the correct per-org alertmanager. The alertmanager applies routing rules, silences, and notification policies before sending notifications.\\n\\n### 5. History Writer (pkg/services/ngalert/state/historian/)\\nThe historian records state transitions for audit and querying. Implementation files:\\n- `core.go`: WriteStateTransition() base function for recording state changes with rule metadata\\n- `annotation.go`: AnnotationBackend uses Grafana annotations as backing store\\n- `prometheus.go`: PrometheusWriter writes state history to Prometheus remote write endpoint\\n- `loki.go`: LokiWriter writes state history to Loki\\n- `multiple.go`: MultipleBackend supports multiple simultaneous backends (e.g., primary Loki + secondary Prometheus)\\n- `backend.go`: Backend type abstraction allowing selection between annotation/prometheus/loki\\n\\nThe Historian interface (persist.go) is called by state manager's persistence layer to Record() state transitions. Multiple backends can be active simultaneously, with one designated as primary for reads.\\n\\n### 6. Alert Sender (pkg/services/ngalert/sender/)\\nThe sender routes evaluated alerts to external systems. Key files:\\n- `router.go`: AlertsRouter created via NewAlertsRouter(). Routes alerts to internal MultiOrgAlertmanager and/or external alertmanagers based on admin configuration\\n- `notifier.go`: ExternalAlertmanagerSender sends alerts to external alertmanagers\\n- `sender.go`: Base sender functionality\\n\\nThe router is called by scheduler with alert transitions and determines whether to send to: (1) internal alertmanager, (2) external alertmanager, or (3) both, based on configuration stored in AdminConfigurationStore.\\n\\n### 7. Main Service Orchestration (pkg/services/ngalert/)\\nThe main files that wire everything together:\\n- `ngalert.go`: AlertNG service class providing ProvideService() dependency injection function that instantiates and wires all components\\n- `evaluation_runner.go`: EvaluationRunner manages the lifecycle of the scheduler during instance startup/shutdown\\n\\n## Data Flow\\n\\n1. **Startup**: ProvideService() creates all components. State manager warm-loads from database via InstanceStore.\\n\\n2. **Rule Evaluation Loop**: EvaluationRunner starts scheduler's Run() method. Scheduler:\\n   - Fetches all active rules via DBstore.GetAlertRulesForScheduling()\\n   - Spawns evaluation goroutine per rule (alert_rule.go)\\n   - At configured intervals, sends evaluation events to each rule's goroutine\\n\\n3. **State Processing**: Each alert_rule goroutine:\\n   - Evaluates the rule (via eval package)\\n   - Sends results to state manager via ProcessEvalResults()\\n   - State manager compares to cached state, determines transitions\\n   - Saves instances to database via InstanceStore.SaveAlertInstances()\\n\\n4. **History Recording**: State manager calls Historian.Record() for all state transitions, which routes to configured backends (annotation/prometheus/loki)\\n\\n5. **Alert Notification**: State manager calls state.Sender (implemented by schedule) which sends firing/resolved alerts to AlertsRouter\\n\\n6. **Alert Routing**: AlertsRouter.Send() determines destination (internal/external/both) and dispatches via:\\n   - Internal: MultiOrgAlertmanager → per-org alertmanager → notification receivers\\n   - External: ExternalAlertmanagerSender → remote alertmanager\\n\\nAll components use consistent models from pkg/services/ngalert/models, maintain prometheus metrics, and support feature toggles via featuremgmt.FeatureToggles.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

subsystem in grafana/grafana comprises five major interacting components:\\n\\n### 1. Alert Rule Storage (pkg/services/ngalert/store/)\\nThe storage layer is implemented by `DBstore` (database.go), a database-backed storage system that persists alert rule definitions and metadata. Key files include:\\n- `database.go`: Main DBstore class implementing AlertingStore and rule persistence\\n- `alert_rule.go`: Methods for querying alert rules via GetAlertRulesForScheduling() and GetAlertRulesKeysForScheduling()\\n- `instance_database.go`: Stores alert instances (individual alert firing states) via SaveAlertInstances() and ListAlertInstances()\\n- `alertmanager.go`: Persists alertmanager configurations\\n\\nThe DBstore is injectable through ProvideDBStore() and serves as the single source of truth for all alert rule definitions across all organizations.\\n\\n### 2. Alert Rule Scheduler (pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/)\\nThe scheduler manages the periodic evaluation of alert rules. Key files:\\n- `schedule.go`: Main scheduler implementing ScheduleService interface, created via NewScheduler(). Manages the evaluation loop and rule registry\\n- `alert_rule.go`: Per-rule executor that runs in its own goroutine, fetches evaluation results and sends them to state manager\\n- `fetcher.go`: updateSchedulableAlertRules() fetches rules from DBstore at configured heartbeat intervals\\n- `recording_rule.go`: Handles recording rules (Prometheus-style rules that write metrics)\\n\\nThe scheduler runs as a continuous service (Run() method) that fetches all active rules, detects changes, and spawns/terminates evaluation goroutines. It uses the AlertsSender interface to dispatch firing alerts.\\n\\n### 3. State Manager (pkg/services/ngalert/state/)\\nThe state manager tracks alert states over time and determines state transitions. Core files:\\n- `manager.go`: Manager class managing alert state cache, created via NewManager(). Implements AlertInstanceManager for state queries\\n- `state.go`: State type representing individual alert instance state with fields like Firing, Pending, etc.\\n- `cache.go`: In-memory cache of all current alert states organized by rule and labels\\n- `persist.go`: StatePersister and Historian interfaces for persistence and history recording\\n- `store_state_reader.go`: StoreStateReader reads alert instances from database on startup\\n\\nThe Manager processes evaluation results via ProcessEvalResults(), compares against previous states to determine transitions (e.g., pending→firing), and records state changes. It maintains a cache warm-loaded from the database (Warm() method) and periodically persists state via StatePersister.\\n\\n### 4. Notifier (pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/)\\nThe notifier delivers alerts to alertmanager instances and manages silences. Key files:\\n- `alertmanager.go`: Per-organization alertmanager wrapper (alertmanager class, NewAlertmanager()). Wraps prometheus-alertmanager\\n- `multiorg_alertmanager.go`: MultiOrgAlertmanager created via NewMultiOrgAlertmanager(). Manages per-org alertmanagers and routes alerts to correct org\\n- `receiver_svc.go`: ReceiverService manages notification receiver configuration per organization\\n- `silence_svc.go`: SilenceService manages active silences that suppress alerts\\n\\nWhen scheduler dispatches alerts, they flow through MultiOrgAlertmanager which routes them to the correct per-org alertmanager. The alertmanager applies routing rules, silences, and notification policies before sending notifications.\\n\\n### 5. History Writer (pkg/services/ngalert/state/historian/)\\nThe historian records state transitions for audit and querying. Implementation files:\\n- `core.go`: WriteStateTransition() base function for recording state changes with rule metadata\\n- `annotation.go`: AnnotationBackend uses Grafana annotations as backing store\\n- `prometheus.go`: PrometheusWriter writes state history to Prometheus remote write endpoint\\n- `loki.go`: LokiWriter writes state history to Loki\\n- `multiple.go`: MultipleBackend supports multiple simultaneous backends (e.g., primary Loki + secondary Prometheus)\\n- `backend.go`: Backend type abstraction allowing selection between annotation/prometheus/loki\\n\\nThe Historian interface (persist.go) is called by state manager's persistence layer to Record() state transitions. Multiple backends can be active simultaneously, with one designated as primary for reads.\\n\\n### 6. Alert Sender (pkg/services/ngalert/sender/)\\nThe sender routes evaluated alerts to external systems. Key files:\\n- `router.go`: AlertsRouter created via NewAlertsRouter(). Routes alerts to internal MultiOrgAlertmanager and/or external alertmanagers based on admin configuration\\n- `notifier.go`: ExternalAlertmanagerSender sends alerts to external alertmanagers\\n- `sender.go`: Base sender functionality\\n\\nThe router is called by scheduler with alert transitions and determines whether to send to: (1) internal alertmanager, (2) external alertmanager, or (3) both, based on configuration stored in AdminConfigurationStore.\\n\\n### 7. Main Service Orchestration (pkg/services/ngalert/)\\nThe main files that wire everything together:\\n- `ngalert.go`: AlertNG service class providing ProvideService() dependency injection function that instantiates and wires all components\\n- `evaluation_runner.go`: EvaluationRunner manages the lifecycle of the scheduler during instance startup/shutdown\\n\\n## Data Flow\\n\\n1. **Startup**: ProvideService() creates all components. State manager warm-loads from database via InstanceStore.\\n\\n2. **Rule Evaluation Loop**: EvaluationRunner starts scheduler's Run() method. Scheduler:\\n   - Fetches all active rules via DBstore.GetAlertRulesForScheduling()\\n   - Spawns evaluation goroutine per rule (alert_rule.go)\\n   - At configured intervals, sends evaluation events to each rule's goroutine\\n\\n3. **State Processing**: Each alert_rule goroutine:\\n   - Evaluates the rule (via eval package)\\n   - Sends results to state manager via ProcessEvalResults()\\n   - State manager compares to cached state, determines transitions\\n   - Saves instances to database via InstanceStore.SaveAlertInstances()\\n\\n4. **History Recording**: State manager calls Historian.Record() for all state transitions, which routes to configured backends (annotation/prometheus/loki)\\n\\n5. **Alert Notification**: State manager calls state.Sender (implemented by schedule) which sends firing/resolved alerts to AlertsRouter\\n\\n6. **Alert Routing**: AlertsRouter.Send() determines destination (internal/external/both) and dispatches via:\\n   - Internal: MultiOrgAlertmanager → per-org alertmanager → notification receivers\\n   - External: ExternalAlertmanagerSender → remote alertmanager\\n\\nAll components use consistent models from pkg/services/ngalert/models, maintain prometheus metrics, and support feature toggles via featuremgmt.FeatureToggles.\"\n    76→}\n    77→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. The alertmanager applies routing rules, silences, and notification policies before sending notifications.\\n\\n### 5. History Writer (pkg/services/ngalert/state/historian/)\\nThe historian records state transitions for audit and querying. Implementation files:\\n- `core.go`: WriteStateTransition() base function for recording state changes with rule metadata\\n- `annotation.go`: AnnotationBackend uses Grafana annotations as backing store\\n- `prometheus.go`: PrometheusWriter writes state history to Prometheus remote write endpoint\\n- `loki.go`: LokiWriter writes state history to Loki\\n- `multiple.go`: MultipleBackend supports multiple simultaneous backends (e.g., primary Loki + secondary Prometheus)\\n- `backend.go`: Backend type abstraction allowing selection between annotation/prometheus/loki\\n\\nThe Historian interface (persist.go) is called by state manager's persistence layer to Record() state transitions. Multiple backends can be active simultaneously, with one designated as primary for reads.\\n\\n### 6. Alert Sender (pkg/services/ngalert/sender/)\\nThe sender routes evaluated alerts to external systems. Key files:\\n- `router.go`: AlertsRouter created via NewAlertsRouter(). Routes alerts to internal MultiOrgAlertmanager and/or external alertmanagers based on admin configuration\\n- `notifier.go`: ExternalAlertmanagerSender sends alerts to external alertmanagers\\n- `sender.go`: Base sender functionality\\n\\nThe router is called by scheduler with alert transitions and determines whether to send to: (1) internal alertmanager, (2) external alertmanager, or (3) both, based on configuration stored in AdminConfigurationStore.\\n\\n### 7. Main Service Orchestration (pkg/services/ngalert/)\\nThe main files that wire everything together:\\n- `ngalert.go`: AlertNG service class providing ProvideService() dependency injection function that instantiates and wires all components\\n- `evaluation_runner.go`: EvaluationRunner manages the lifecycle of the scheduler during instance startup/shutdown\\n\\n## Data Flow\\n\\n1. **Startup**: ProvideService() creates all components. State manager warm-loads from database via InstanceStore.\\n\\n2. **Rule Evaluation Loop**: EvaluationRunner starts scheduler's Run() method. Scheduler:\\n   - Fetches all active rules via DBstore.GetAlertRulesForScheduling()\\n   - Spawns evaluation goroutine per rule (alert_rule.go)\\n   - At configured intervals, sends evaluation events to each rule's goroutine\\n\\n3. **State Processing**: Each alert_rule goroutine:\\n   - Evaluates the rule (via eval package)\\n   - Sends results to state manager via ProcessEvalResults()\\n   - State manager compares to cached state, determines transitions\\n   - Saves instances to database via InstanceStore.SaveAlertInstances()\\n\\n4. **History Recording**: State manager calls Historian.Record() for all state transitions, which routes to configured backends (annotation/prometheus/loki)\\n\\n5. **Alert Notification**: State manager calls state.Sender (implemented by schedule) which sends firing/resolved alerts to AlertsRouter\\n\\n6. **Alert Routing**: AlertsRouter.Send() determines destination (internal/external/both) and dispatches via:\\n   - Internal: MultiOrgAlertmanager → per-org alertmanager → notification receivers\\n   - External: ExternalAlertmanagerSender → remote alertmanager\\n\\nAll components use consistent models from pkg/services/ngalert/models, maintain prometheus metrics, and support feature toggles via featuremgmt.FeatureToggles.\"\n}\n","numLines":77,"startLine":1,"totalLines":77}}}
